The key components are:\\n24: * `GrpcMuxImpl` which manages the xDS transport and multiplexing one or more subscriptions on a\\n25:   single gRPC stream. The key components are:\n24: * `GrpcMuxImpl` which manages the xDS transport and multiplexing one or more subscriptions on a\n25:   single gRPC stream. The muxer is responsible for managing the wire level concerns via\n26:   `GrpcStream`, while also tracking subscription state and watchers for updates. Multiple resource\n27:   type URLs may be managed by a single muxer. For non-ADS, this will always be one stream per\n28:   subscription, whereas for ADS, multiple subscriptions will be multiplexed on a single stream.\n29: * `SubscriptionState` tracks subscription state for a single resource type URL.\n30: * `WatchMap` tracks all the subscribers for a given resource type.\n31: * Each Envoy subsystem, e.g. LDS, CDS, etc. has a `GrpcSubscriptionImpl` that points at a `GrpcMuxImpl`.\n32: \n33: The above components are responsible for subscriptions, watches, muxing and stream management.\n34: Caching is not currently a centralized service, and is instead delegated to per-resource type\n35: ","endLine":35,"startLine":23},{"content":"78: \n79: Aggregated means that EDS, CDS, etc resources are all carried by the same gRPC stream.\n80: For Envoy's implementation of xDS client logic, there is effectively no difference\n81: between aggregated xDS and non-aggregated: they both use the same request/response protos. **GrpcMux interface** (envoy/config/grpc_mux.h) defines the abstract interface for managing gRPC subscriptions to xDS APIs. It supports multiplexing multiple resource types over a single gRPC stream for ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service).\\n\\n## Legacy Implementations\\n\\n**GrpcSubscriptionImpl** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_impl.h/.cc) is the primary adapter that bridges the xDS transport layer with Envoy's configuration subscription interface. It manages subscriptions for individual resource types and handles callbacks from the mux implementations. GrpcCollectionSubscriptionImpl extends this for collection resources.\\n\\n**GrpcMuxImpl** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_mux_impl.h/.cc) implements the State-of-the-World (SotW) xDS protocol. It manages the gRPC stream lifecycle, multiplexes multiple resource types, and uses DeltaSubscriptionState for tracking protocol state. This is the legacy SotW implementation.\\n\\n**NewGrpcMuxImpl** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/new_grpc_mux_impl.h/.cc) implements the Delta xDS protocol variant, which sends only resource changes rather than the complete state. It manages subscriptions per resource type and tracks updates more efficiently for large datasets.\\n\\n**GrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory** and **DeltaGrpcConfigSubscriptionFactory** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/grpc_subscription_factory.h/.cc) are factory classes that select between SotW and Delta modes based on configuration. They instantiate the appropriate mux implementation and wrap it with GrpcSubscriptionImpl.\\n\\n## Unified XdsMux Implementation\\n\\nThe xds_mux subdirectory contains a unified, templated implementation replacing the legacy split:\\n\\n**GrpcMuxImpl template** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.h/.cc) is a template class parameterized on subscription state type (S), state factory (F), and request/response message types. This single implementation supports both SotW and Delta through template specialization.\\n\\n**GrpcMuxSotw** and **GrpcMuxDelta** are concrete template instantiations:\\n- GrpcMuxSotw uses SotwSubscriptionState with DiscoveryRequest/DiscoveryResponse\\n- GrpcMuxDelta uses DeltaSubscriptionState with DeltaDiscoveryRequest/DeltaDiscoveryResponse\\n\\n**SubscriptionState hierarchy** (source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/xds_mux/subscription_state.h):\\n- SubscriptionState is the base marker class\\n- BaseSubscriptionState<RS, RQ> is the template base for protocol state tracking\\n- **SotwSubscriptionState** (sotw_subscription_state.h/.cc) tracks full state updates per resource type\\n- **DeltaSubscriptionState** (delta_subscription_state.h/.cc) tracks incremental updates with resource versioning\\n- Both use **SotwSubscriptionStateFactory** and **DeltaSubscriptionStateFactory** respectively\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**WatchMap** (watch_map.h/.cc) maintains the watches-to-subscription mapping, delivering updates to all interested watchers for a given resource type.\\n\\n**GrpcMuxContext** (grpc_mux_context.h) is a struct containing all parameters needed to create GrpcMux objects: async client, dispatcher, service method descriptor, local info, rate limiting settings, and resource caches.\\n\\n**GrpcStreamInterface** (grpc_stream_interface.h) defines the low-level gRPC stream interface for sending/receiving xDS messages.\\n\\n**GrpcMuxFailover** (grpc_mux_failover.h) implements failover between primary and failover xDS config sources.\\n\\n**NullGrpcMuxImpl** (source/common/config/null_grpc_mux_impl.h) is a no-op implementation used when ADS is not configured.\\n\\nThe legacy delta_subscription_state.h/.cc in the parent directory provides the original Delta implementation used by NewGrpcMuxImpl before the unified template was introduced.\\n\\nThe migration from legacy (GrpcMuxImpl/NewGrpcMuxImpl + separate state classes) to unified (templated GrpcMuxImpl with GrpcMuxSotw/GrpcMuxDelta) is controlled by the runtime feature \\\"envoy.reloadable_features.unified_mux\\\" in grpc_subscription_factory.cc.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2555,"cache_read_input_tokens":77544,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2555},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"de377493-6079-48d5-b98c-47d3b3a33845","uuid":"c6e1369c-862d-4064-9b37-697c888b78d7"}
